    13	func RichParameter(inv *serpent.Invocation, templateVersionParameter codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter, defaultOverrides map[string]string) (string, error) {
    14	        label := templateVersionParameter.Name
    15	        if templateVersionParameter.DisplayName != "" {
    16	                label = templateVersionParameter.DisplayName
    17	        }
    18	
    19	        if templateVersionParameter.Ephemeral {
    20	                label += pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Warn, " (build option)")
    21	        }
    22	
    23	        _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout, Bold(label))
    24	
    25	        if templateVersionParameter.DescriptionPlaintext != "" {
    26	                _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout, "  "+strings.TrimSpace(strings.Join(strings.Split(templateVersionParameter.DescriptionPlaintext, "\n"), "\n  "))+"\n")
    27	        }
    28	
    29	        defaultValue := templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue
    30	        if v, ok := defaultOverrides[templateVersionParameter.Name]; ok {
    31	                defaultValue = v
    32	        }
    33	
    34	        var err error
    35	        var value string
    36	        switch {
    37	        case templateVersionParameter.Type == "list(string)":
    38	                // Move the cursor up a single line for nicer display!
    39	                _, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")
    40	
    41	                var options []string
    42	                err = json.Unmarshal([]byte(templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue), &options)
    43	                if err != nil {
    44	                        return "", err
    45	                }
    46	
    47	                values, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{
    48	                        Options:  options,
    49	                        Defaults: options,
    50	                })
    51	                if err == nil {
    52	                        v, err := json.Marshal(&values)
    53	                        if err != nil {
    54	                                return "", err
    55	                        }
    56	
    57	                        _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
    58	                        pretty.Fprintf(
    59	                                inv.Stdout,
    60	                                DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%s\n", strings.Join(values, ", "),
    61	                        )
    62	                        value = string(v)
    63	                }
    64	        case len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0:
    65	                // Move the cursor up a single line for nicer display!
    66	                _, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")
    67	                var richParameterOption *codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption
    68	                richParameterOption, err = RichSelect(inv, RichSelectOptions{
    69	                        Options:    templateVersionParameter.Options,
    70	                        Default:    defaultValue,
    71	                        HideSearch: true,
    72	                })
    73	                if err == nil {
    74	                        _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
    75	                        pretty.Fprintf(inv.Stdout, DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%s\n", richParameterOption.Name)
    76	                        value = richParameterOption.Value
    77	                }
    78	        default:
    79	                text := "Enter a value"
    80	                if !templateVersionParameter.Required {
    81	                        text += fmt.Sprintf(" (default: %q)", defaultValue)
    82	                }
    83	                text += ":"
    84	
    85	                value, err = Prompt(inv, PromptOptions{
    86	                        Text: Bold(text),
    87	                        Validate: func(value string) error {
    88	                                return validateRichPrompt(value, templateVersionParameter)
    89	                        },
    90	                })
    91	                value = strings.TrimSpace(value)
    92	        }
    93	        if err != nil {
    94	                return "", err
    95	        }
    96	
    97	        // If they didn't specify anything, use the default value if set.
    98	        if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) == 0 && value == "" {
    99	                value = defaultValue
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        return value, nil
   103	}
   104	
   105	func validateRichPrompt(value string, p codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter) error {
   106	        return codersdk.ValidateWorkspaceBuildParameter(p, &codersdk.WorkspaceBuildParameter{
   107	                Name:  p.Name,
   108	                Value: value,
   109	        }, nil)
   110	}

     1	package cliui
     2	
     3	import (
     4	        "flag"
     5	        "fmt"
     6	        "os"
     7	        "os/signal"
     8	        "strings"
     9	        "syscall"
    10	
    11	        "github.com/charmbracelet/bubbles/textinput"
    12	        tea "github.com/charmbracelet/bubbletea"
    13	        "golang.org/x/xerrors"
    14	
    15	        "github.com/coder/coder/v2/codersdk"
    16	        "github.com/coder/pretty"
    17	        "github.com/coder/serpent"
    18	)
    19	
    20	const defaultSelectModelHeight = 7
    21	
    22	type terminateMsg struct{}
    23	
    24	func installSignalHandler(p *tea.Program) func() {
    25	        ch := make(chan struct{})
    26	
    27	        go func() {
    28	                sig := make(chan os.Signal, 1)
    29	                signal.Notify(sig, os.Interrupt, syscall.SIGTERM)
    30	
    31	                defer func() {
    32	                        signal.Stop(sig)
    33	                        close(ch)
    34	                }()
    35	
    36	                for {
    37	                        select {
    38	                        case <-ch:
    39	                                return
    40	
    41	                        case <-sig:
    42	                                p.Send(terminateMsg{})
    43	                        }
    44	                }
    45	        }()
    46	
    47	        return func() {
    48	                ch <- struct{}{}
    49	        }
    50	}
    51	
    52	type SelectOptions struct {
    53	        Options []string
    54	        // Default will be highlighted first if it's a valid option.
    55	        Default    string
    56	        Message    string
    57	        Size       int
    58	        HideSearch bool
    59	}
    60	
    61	type RichSelectOptions struct {
    62	        Options    []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption
    63	        Default    string
    64	        Size       int
    65	        HideSearch bool
    66	}
    67	
    68	// RichSelect displays a list of user options including name and description.
    69	func RichSelect(inv *serpent.Invocation, richOptions RichSelectOptions) (*codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption, error) {
    70	        opts := make([]string, len(richOptions.Options))
    71	        var defaultOpt string
    72	        for i, option := range richOptions.Options {
    73	                line := option.Name
    74	                if len(option.Description) > 0 {
    75	                        line += ": " + option.Description
    76	                }
    77	                opts[i] = line
    78	
    79	                if option.Value == richOptions.Default {
    80	                        defaultOpt = line
    81	                }
    82	        }
    83	
    84	        selected, err := Select(inv, SelectOptions{
    85	                Options:    opts,
    86	                Default:    defaultOpt,
    87	                Size:       richOptions.Size,
    88	                HideSearch: richOptions.HideSearch,
    89	        })
    90	        if err != nil {
    91	                return nil, err
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        for i, option := range opts {
    95	                if option == selected {
    96	                        return &richOptions.Options[i], nil
    97	                }
    98	        }
    99	        return nil, xerrors.Errorf("unknown option selected: %s", selected)
   100	}
   101	
   102	// Select displays a list of user options.
   103	func Select(inv *serpent.Invocation, opts SelectOptions) (string, error) {
   104	        // The survey library used *always* fails when testing on Windows,
   105	        // as it requires a live TTY (can't be a conpty). We should fork
   106	        // this library to add a dummy fallback, that simply reads/writes
   107	        // to the IO provided. See:
   108	        // https://github.com/AlecAivazis/survey/blob/master/terminal/runereader_windows.go#L94
   109	        if flag.Lookup("test.v") != nil {
   110	                return opts.Options[0], nil
   111	        }
   112	
   113	        initialModel := selectModel{
   114	                search:     textinput.New(),
   115	                hideSearch: opts.HideSearch,
   116	                options:    opts.Options,
   117	                height:     opts.Size,
   118	                message:    opts.Message,
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        if initialModel.height == 0 {
   122	                initialModel.height = defaultSelectModelHeight
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        initialModel.search.Prompt = ""
   126	        initialModel.search.Focus()
   127	
   128	        p := tea.NewProgram(
   129	                initialModel,
   130	                tea.WithoutSignalHandler(),
   131	                tea.WithContext(inv.Context()),
   132	                tea.WithInput(inv.Stdin),
   133	                tea.WithOutput(inv.Stdout),
   134	        )
   135	
   136	        closeSignalHandler := installSignalHandler(p)
   137	        defer closeSignalHandler()
   138	
   139	        m, err := p.Run()
   140	        if err != nil {
   141	                return "", err
   142	        }
   143	
   144	        model, ok := m.(selectModel)
   145	        if !ok {
   146	                return "", xerrors.New(fmt.Sprintf("unknown model found %T (%+v)", m, m))
   147	        }
   148	
   149	        if model.canceled {
   150	                return "", ErrCanceled
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        return model.selected, nil
   154	}
   155	
   156	type selectModel struct {
   157	        search     textinput.Model
   158	        options    []string
   159	        cursor     int
   160	        height     int
   161	        message    string
   162	        selected   string
   163	        canceled   bool
   164	        hideSearch bool
   165	}
   166	
   167	func (selectModel) Init() tea.Cmd {
   168	        return nil
   169	}
   170	
   171	//nolint:revive // The linter complains about modifying 'm' but this is typical practice for bubbletea
   172	func (m selectModel) Update(msg tea.Msg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   173	        var cmd tea.Cmd
   174	
   175	        switch msg := msg.(type) {
   176	        case terminateMsg:
   177	                m.canceled = true
   178	                return m, tea.Quit
   179	
   180	        case tea.KeyMsg:
   181	                switch msg.Type {
   182	                case tea.KeyCtrlC:
   183	                        m.canceled = true
   184	                        return m, tea.Quit
   185	
   186	                case tea.KeyEnter:
   187	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   188	                        if len(options) != 0 {
   189	                                m.selected = options[m.cursor]
   190	                                return m, tea.Quit
   191	                        }
   192	
   193	                case tea.KeyUp:
   194	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   195	                        if m.cursor > 0 {
   196	                                m.cursor--
   197	                        } else {
   198	                                m.cursor = len(options) - 1
   199	                        }
   200	
   201	                case tea.KeyDown:
   202	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   203	                        if m.cursor < len(options)-1 {
   204	                                m.cursor++
   205	                        } else {
   206	                                m.cursor = 0
   207	                        }
   208	                }
   209	        }
   210	
   211	        if !m.hideSearch {
   212	                oldSearch := m.search.Value()
   213	                m.search, cmd = m.search.Update(msg)
   214	
   215	                // If the search query has changed then we need to ensure
   216	                // the cursor is still pointing at a valid option.
   217	                if m.search.Value() != oldSearch {
   218	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   219	
   220	                        if m.cursor > len(options)-1 {
   221	                                m.cursor = max(0, len(options)-1)
   222	                        }
   223	                }
   224	        }
   225	
   226	        return m, cmd
   227	}
   228	
   229	func (m selectModel) View() string {
   230	        var s strings.Builder
   231	
   232	        msg := pretty.Sprintf(pretty.Bold(), "? %s", m.message)
   233	
   234	        if m.selected != "" {
   235	                selected := pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, m.selected)
   236	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s %s\n", msg, selected))
   237	
   238	                return s.String()
   239	        }
   240	
   241	        if m.hideSearch {
   242	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s [Use arrows to move]\n", msg))
   243	        } else {
   244	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(
   245	                        "%s %s[Use arrows to move, type to filter]\n",
   246	                        msg,
   247	                        m.search.View(),
   248	                ))
   249	        }
   250	
   251	        options, start := m.viewableOptions()
   252	
   253	        for i, option := range options {
   254	                // Is this the currently selected option?
   255	                style := pretty.Wrap("  ", "")
   256	                if m.cursor == start+i {
   257	                        style = pretty.Style{
   258	                                pretty.Wrap("> ", ""),
   259	                                DefaultStyles.Keyword,
   260	                        }
   261	                }
   262	
   263	                _, _ = s.WriteString(pretty.Sprint(style, option))
   264	                _, _ = s.WriteString("\n")
   265	        }
   266	
   267	        return s.String()
   268	}
   269	
   270	func (m selectModel) viewableOptions() ([]string, int) {
   271	        options := m.filteredOptions()
   272	        halfHeight := m.height / 2
   273	        bottom := 0
   274	        top := len(options)
   275	
   276	        switch {
   277	        case m.cursor <= halfHeight:
   278	                top = min(top, m.height)
   279	        case m.cursor < top-halfHeight:
   280	                bottom = max(0, m.cursor-halfHeight)
   281	                top = min(top, m.cursor+halfHeight+1)
   282	        default:
   283	                bottom = max(0, top-m.height)
   284	        }
   285	
   286	        return options[bottom:top], bottom
   287	}
   288	
   289	func (m selectModel) filteredOptions() []string {
   290	        options := []string{}
   291	        for _, o := range m.options {
   292	                filter := strings.ToLower(m.search.Value())
   293	                option := strings.ToLower(o)
   294	
   295	                if strings.Contains(option, filter) {
   296	                        options = append(options, o)
   297	                }
   298	        }
   299	        return options
   300	}
   301	
   302	type MultiSelectOptions struct {
   303	        Message           string
   304	        Options           []string
   305	        Defaults          []string
   306	        EnableCustomInput bool
   307	}
   308	
   309	func MultiSelect(inv *serpent.Invocation, opts MultiSelectOptions) ([]string, error) {
   310	        // Similar hack is applied to Select()
   311	        if flag.Lookup("test.v") != nil {
   312	                return opts.Defaults, nil
   313	        }
   314	
   315	        options := make([]*multiSelectOption, len(opts.Options))
   316	        for i, option := range opts.Options {
   317	                chosen := false
   318	                for _, d := range opts.Defaults {
   319	                        if option == d {
   320	                                chosen = true
   321	                                break
   322	                        }
   323	                }
   324	
   325	                options[i] = &multiSelectOption{
   326	                        option: option,
   327	                        chosen: chosen,
   328	                }
   329	        }
   330	
   331	        initialModel := multiSelectModel{
   332	                search:            textinput.New(),
   333	                options:           options,
   334	                message:           opts.Message,
   335	                enableCustomInput: opts.EnableCustomInput,
   336	        }
   337	
   338	        initialModel.search.Prompt = ""
   339	        initialModel.search.Focus()
   340	
   341	        p := tea.NewProgram(
   342	                initialModel,
   343	                tea.WithoutSignalHandler(),
   344	                tea.WithContext(inv.Context()),
   345	                tea.WithInput(inv.Stdin),
   346	                tea.WithOutput(inv.Stdout),
   347	        )
   348	
   349	        closeSignalHandler := installSignalHandler(p)
   350	        defer closeSignalHandler()
   351	
   352	        m, err := p.Run()
   353	        if err != nil {
   354	                return nil, err
   355	        }
   356	
   357	        model, ok := m.(multiSelectModel)
   358	        if !ok {
   359	                return nil, xerrors.New(fmt.Sprintf("unknown model found %T (%+v)", m, m))
   360	        }
   361	
   362	        if model.canceled {
   363	                return nil, ErrCanceled
   364	        }
   365	
   366	        return model.selectedOptions(), nil
   367	}
   368	
   369	type multiSelectOption struct {
   370	        option string
   371	        chosen bool
   372	}
   373	
   374	type multiSelectModel struct {
   375	        search            textinput.Model
   376	        options           []*multiSelectOption
   377	        cursor            int
   378	        message           string
   379	        canceled          bool
   380	        selected          bool
   381	        isCustomInputMode bool   // track if we're adding a custom option
   382	        customInput       string // store custom input
   383	        enableCustomInput bool   // control whether custom input is allowed
   384	}
   385	
   386	func (multiSelectModel) Init() tea.Cmd {
   387	        return nil
   388	}
   389	
   390	//nolint:revive // For same reason as previous Update definition
   391	func (m multiSelectModel) Update(msg tea.Msg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   392	        var cmd tea.Cmd
   393	
   394	        if m.isCustomInputMode {
   395	                return m.handleCustomInputMode(msg)
   396	        }
   397	
   398	        switch msg := msg.(type) {
   399	        case terminateMsg:
   400	                m.canceled = true
   401	                return m, tea.Quit
   402	
   403	        case tea.KeyMsg:
   404	                switch msg.Type {
   405	                case tea.KeyCtrlC:
   406	                        m.canceled = true
   407	                        return m, tea.Quit
   408	
   409	                case tea.KeyEnter:
   410	                        // Switch to custom input mode if we're on the "+ Add custom value:" option
   411	                        if m.enableCustomInput && m.cursor == len(m.filteredOptions()) {
   412	                                m.isCustomInputMode = true
   413	                                return m, nil
   414	                        }
   415	                        if len(m.options) != 0 {
   416	                                m.selected = true
   417	                                return m, tea.Quit
   418	                        }
   419	
   420	                case tea.KeySpace:
   421	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   422	                        if len(options) != 0 {
   423	                                options[m.cursor].chosen = !options[m.cursor].chosen
   424	                        }
   425	                        // We back out early here otherwise a space will be inserted
   426	                        // into the search field.
   427	                        return m, nil
   428	
   429	                case tea.KeyUp:
   430	                        maxIndex := m.getMaxIndex()
   431	                        if m.cursor > 0 {
   432	                                m.cursor--
   433	                        } else {
   434	                                m.cursor = maxIndex
   435	                        }
   436	
   437	                case tea.KeyDown:
   438	                        maxIndex := m.getMaxIndex()
   439	                        if m.cursor < maxIndex {
   440	                                m.cursor++
   441	                        } else {
   442	                                m.cursor = 0
   443	                        }
   444	
   445	                case tea.KeyRight:
   446	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   447	                        for _, option := range options {
   448	                                option.chosen = true
   449	                        }
   450	
   451	                case tea.KeyLeft:
   452	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   453	                        for _, option := range options {
   454	                                option.chosen = false
   455	                        }
   456	                }
   457	        }
   458	
   459	        oldSearch := m.search.Value()
   460	        m.search, cmd = m.search.Update(msg)
   461	
   462	        // If the search query has changed then we need to ensure
   463	        // the cursor is still pointing at a valid option.
   464	        if m.search.Value() != oldSearch {
   465	                options := m.filteredOptions()
   466	                if m.cursor > len(options)-1 {
   467	                        m.cursor = max(0, len(options)-1)
   468	                }
   469	        }
   470	
   471	        return m, cmd
   472	}
   473	
   474	func (m multiSelectModel) getMaxIndex() int {
   475	        options := m.filteredOptions()
   476	        if m.enableCustomInput {
   477	                // Include the "+ Add custom value" entry
   478	                return len(options)
   479	        }
   480	        // Includes only the actual options
   481	        return len(options) - 1
   482	}
   483	
   484	// handleCustomInputMode manages keyboard interactions when in custom input mode
   485	func (m *multiSelectModel) handleCustomInputMode(msg tea.Msg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   486	        keyMsg, ok := msg.(tea.KeyMsg)
   487	        if !ok {
   488	                return m, nil
   489	        }
   490	
   491	        switch keyMsg.Type {
   492	        case tea.KeyEnter:
   493	                return m.handleCustomInputSubmission()
   494	
   495	        case tea.KeyCtrlC:
   496	                m.canceled = true
   497	                return m, tea.Quit
   498	
   499	        case tea.KeyBackspace:
   500	                return m.handleCustomInputBackspace()
   501	
   502	        default:
   503	                m.customInput += keyMsg.String()
   504	                return m, nil
   505	        }
   506	}
   507	
   508	// handleCustomInputSubmission processes the submission of custom input
   509	func (m *multiSelectModel) handleCustomInputSubmission() (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   510	        if m.customInput == "" {
   511	                m.isCustomInputMode = false
   512	                return m, nil
   513	        }
   514	
   515	        // Clear search to ensure option is visible and cursor points to the new option
   516	        m.search.SetValue("")
   517	
   518	        // Check for duplicates
   519	        for i, opt := range m.options {
   520	                if opt.option == m.customInput {
   521	                        // If the option exists but isn't chosen, select it
   522	                        if !opt.chosen {
   523	                                opt.chosen = true
   524	                        }
   525	
   526	                        // Point cursor to the new option
   527	                        m.cursor = i
   528	
   529	                        // Reset custom input mode to disabled
   530	                        m.isCustomInputMode = false
   531	                        m.customInput = ""
   532	                        return m, nil
   533	                }
   534	        }
   535	
   536	        // Add new unique option
   537	        m.options = append(m.options, &multiSelectOption{
   538	                option: m.customInput,
   539	                chosen: true,
   540	        })
   541	
   542	        // Point cursor to the newly added option
   543	        m.cursor = len(m.options) - 1
   544	
   545	        // Reset custom input mode to disabled
   546	        m.customInput = ""
   547	        m.isCustomInputMode = false
   548	        return m, nil
   549	}
   550	
   551	// handleCustomInputBackspace handles backspace in custom input mode
   552	func (m *multiSelectModel) handleCustomInputBackspace() (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   553	        if len(m.customInput) > 0 {
   554	                m.customInput = m.customInput[:len(m.customInput)-1]
   555	        }
   556	        return m, nil
   557	}
   558	
   559	func (m multiSelectModel) View() string {
   560	        var s strings.Builder
   561	
   562	        msg := pretty.Sprintf(pretty.Bold(), "? %s", m.message)
   563	
   564	        if m.selected {
   565	                selected := pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, strings.Join(m.selectedOptions(), ", "))
   566	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s %s\n", msg, selected))
   567	
   568	                return s.String()
   569	        }
   570	
   571	        if m.isCustomInputMode {
   572	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s\nEnter custom value: %s\n", msg, m.customInput))
   573	                return s.String()
   574	        }
   575	
   576	        _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(
   577	                "%s %s[Use arrows to move, space to select, <right> to all, <left> to none, type to filter]\n",
   578	                msg,
   579	                m.search.View(),
   580	        ))
   581	
   582	        options := m.filteredOptions()
   583	        for i, option := range options {
   584	                cursor := "  "
   585	                chosen := "[ ]"
   586	                o := option.option
   587	
   588	                if m.cursor == i {
   589	                        cursor = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, "> ")
   590	                        chosen = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, "[ ]")
   591	                        o = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, o)
   592	                }
   593	
   594	                if option.chosen {
   595	                        chosen = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, "[x]")
   596	                }
   597	
   598	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(
   599	                        "%s%s %s\n",
   600	                        cursor,
   601	                        chosen,
   602	                        o,
   603	                ))
   604	        }
   605	
   606	        if m.enableCustomInput {
   607	                // Add the "+ Add custom value" option at the bottom
   608	                cursor := "  "
   609	                text := " + Add custom value"
   610	                if m.cursor == len(options) {
   611	                        cursor = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, "> ")
   612	                        text = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, text)
   613	                }
   614	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s%s\n", cursor, text))
   615	        }
   616	        return s.String()
   617	}
   618	
   619	func (m multiSelectModel) filteredOptions() []*multiSelectOption {
   620	        options := []*multiSelectOption{}
   621	        for _, o := range m.options {
   622	                filter := strings.ToLower(m.search.Value())
   623	                option := strings.ToLower(o.option)
   624	
   625	                if strings.Contains(option, filter) {
   626	                        options = append(options, o)
   627	                }
   628	        }
   629	        return options
   630	}
   631	
   632	func (m multiSelectModel) selectedOptions() []string {
   633	        selected := []string{}
   634	        for _, o := range m.options {
   635	                if o.chosen {
   636	                        selected = append(selected, o.option)
   637	                }
   638	        }
   639	        return selected
   640	}

    69	// WeekdaysToBitmap converts a list of weekdays to a bitmap in accordance with
    70	// the schedule package's rules. The 0th bit is Monday, ..., the 6th bit is
    71	// Sunday. The 7th bit is unused.
    72	func WeekdaysToBitmap(days []string) (uint8, error) {
    73	        var bitmap uint8
    74	        for _, day := range days {
    75	                switch strings.ToLower(day) {
    76	                case "monday":
    77	                        bitmap |= 1 << 0
    78	                case "tuesday":
    79	                        bitmap |= 1 << 1
    80	                case "wednesday":
    81	                        bitmap |= 1 << 2
    82	                case "thursday":
    83	                        bitmap |= 1 << 3
    84	                case "friday":
    85	                        bitmap |= 1 << 4
    86	                case "saturday":
    87	                        bitmap |= 1 << 5
    88	                case "sunday":
    89	                        bitmap |= 1 << 6
    90	                default:
    91	                        return 0, xerrors.Errorf("invalid weekday %q", day)
    92	                }
    93	        }
    94	        return bitmap, nil
    95	}
    96	
    97	// BitmapToWeekdays converts a bitmap to a list of weekdays in accordance with
    98	// the schedule package's rules (see above).
    99	func BitmapToWeekdays(bitmap uint8) []string {
   100	        days := []string{}
   101	        for i := 0; i < 7; i++ {
   102	                if bitmap&(1<<i) != 0 {
   103	                        switch i {
   104	                        case 0:
   105	                                days = append(days, "monday")
   106	                        case 1:
   107	                                days = append(days, "tuesday")
   108	                        case 2:
   109	                                days = append(days, "wednesday")
   110	                        case 3:
   111	                                days = append(days, "thursday")
   112	                        case 4:
   113	                                days = append(days, "friday")
   114	                        case 5:
   115	                                days = append(days, "saturday")
   116	                        case 6:
   117	                                days = append(days, "sunday")
   118	                        }
   119	                }
   120	        }
   121	        return days
   122	}
   123	
   124	var AllDaysOfWeek = []string{"monday", "tuesday", "wednesday", "thursday", "friday", "saturday", "sunday"}

   126	type TemplateAutostartRequirement struct {
   127	        // DaysOfWeek is a list of days of the week in which autostart is allowed
   128	        // to happen. If no days are specified, autostart is not allowed.
   129	        DaysOfWeek []string `json:"days_of_week" enums:"monday,tuesday,wednesday,thursday,friday,saturday,sunday"`
   130	}
   131	
   132	type TemplateAutostopRequirement struct {
   133	        // DaysOfWeek is a list of days of the week on which restarts are required.
   134	        // Restarts happen within the user's quiet hours (in their configured
   135	        // timezone). If no days are specified, restarts are not required. Weekdays
   136	        // cannot be specified twice.
   137	        //
   138	        // Restarts will only happen on weekdays in this list on weeks which line up
   139	        // with Weeks.
   140	        DaysOfWeek []string `json:"days_of_week" enums:"monday,tuesday,wednesday,thursday,friday,saturday,sunday"`
   141	        // Weeks is the number of weeks between required restarts. Weeks are synced
   142	        // across all workspaces (and Coder deployments) using modulo math on a
   143	        // hardcoded epoch week of January 2nd, 2023 (the first Monday of 2023).
   144	        // Values of 0 or 1 indicate weekly restarts. Values of 2 indicate
   145	        // fortnightly restarts, etc.
   146	        Weeks int64 `json:"weeks"`
   147	}

   276	func (c *Client) Template(ctx context.Context, template uuid.UUID) (Template, error) {
   277	        res, err := c.Request(ctx, http.MethodGet, fmt.Sprintf("/api/v2/templates/%s", template), nil)
   278	        if err != nil {
   279	                return Template{}, xerrors.Errorf("do request: %w", err)
   280	        }
   281	        defer res.Body.Close()
   282	        if res.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
   283	                return Template{}, ReadBodyAsError(res)
   284	        }
   285	        var resp Template
   286	        return resp, json.NewDecoder(res.Body).Decode(&resp)
   287	}

   133	        }
   134	        inv := cmd.Invoke()
   135	        ptty.Attach(inv)
   136	        return values, inv.Run()

    22	// PromptOptions supply a set of options to the prompt.
    23	type PromptOptions struct {
    24	        Text    string
    25	        Default string
    26	        // When true, the input will be masked with asterisks.
    27	        Secret    bool
    28	        IsConfirm bool
    29	        Validate  func(string) error

    32	const skipPromptFlag = "yes"
    33	
    34	// SkipPromptOption adds a "--yes/-y" flag to the cmd that can be used to skip
    35	// prompts.
    36	func SkipPromptOption() serpent.Option {
    37	        return serpent.Option{
    38	                Flag:          skipPromptFlag,
    39	                FlagShorthand: "y",
    40	                Description:   "Bypass prompts.",
    41	                // Discard
    42	                Value: serpent.BoolOf(new(bool)),
    43	        }
    44	}
    45	
    46	const (
    47	        ConfirmYes = "yes"
    48	        ConfirmNo  = "no"
    49	)
    50	
    51	// Prompt asks the user for input.
    52	func Prompt(inv *serpent.Invocation, opts PromptOptions) (string, error) {
    53	        // If the cmd has a "yes" flag for skipping confirm prompts, honor it.
    54	        // If it's not a "Confirm" prompt, then don't skip. As the default value of
    55	        // "yes" makes no sense.
    56	        if opts.IsConfirm && inv.ParsedFlags().Lookup(skipPromptFlag) != nil {
    57	                if skip, _ := inv.ParsedFlags().GetBool(skipPromptFlag); skip {
    58	                        return ConfirmYes, nil
    59	                }
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        pretty.Fprintf(inv.Stdout, DefaultStyles.FocusedPrompt, "")
    63	        pretty.Fprintf(inv.Stdout, pretty.Nop, "%s ", opts.Text)
    64	        if opts.IsConfirm {
    65	                if len(opts.Default) == 0 {
    66	                        opts.Default = ConfirmYes
    67	                }
    68	                var (
    69	                        renderedYes = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Placeholder, ConfirmYes)
    70	                        renderedNo  = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Placeholder, ConfirmNo)
    71	                )
    72	                if opts.Default == ConfirmYes {
    73	                        renderedYes = Bold(ConfirmYes)
    74	                } else {
    75	                        renderedNo = Bold(ConfirmNo)
    76	                }
    77	                _, _ = fmt.Fprintf(inv.Stdout, "(%s/%s) ", renderedYes, renderedNo)
    78	        } else if opts.Default != "" {
    79	                _, _ = fmt.Fprintf(inv.Stdout, "(%s) ", pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Placeholder, opts.Default))
    80	        }
    81	        interrupt := make(chan os.Signal, 1)
    82	
    83	        if inv.Stdin == nil {
    84	                panic("inv.Stdin is nil")
    85	        }
    86	
    87	        errCh := make(chan error, 1)
    88	        lineCh := make(chan string)
    89	
    90	        go func() {
    91	                var line string
    92	                var err error
    93	
    94	                signal.Notify(interrupt, os.Interrupt)
    95	                defer signal.Stop(interrupt)
    96	
    97	                inFile, isInputFile := inv.Stdin.(*os.File)
    98	                if opts.Secret && isInputFile && isatty.IsTerminal(inFile.Fd()) {
    99	                        line, err = readSecretInput(inFile, inv.Stdout)
   100	                } else {
   101	                        line, err = readUntil(inv.Stdin, '\n')
   102	
   103	                        // Check if the first line beings with JSON object or array chars.
   104	                        // This enables multiline JSON to be pasted into an input, and have
   105	                        // it parse properly.
   106	                        if err == nil && (strings.HasPrefix(line, "{") || strings.HasPrefix(line, "[")) {
   107	                                line, err = promptJSON(inv.Stdin, line)
   108	                        }
   109	                }
   110	                if err != nil {
   111	                        errCh <- err
   112	                        return
   113	                }
   114	                line = strings.TrimRight(line, "\r\n")
   115	                if line == "" {
   116	                        line = opts.Default
   117	                }
   118	                select {
   119	                case <-inv.Context().Done():
   120	                case lineCh <- line:
   121	                }
   122	        }()
   123	
   124	        select {
   125	        case err := <-errCh:
   126	                return "", err
   127	        case line := <-lineCh:
   128	                if opts.IsConfirm && line != "yes" && line != "y" {
   129	                        return line, xerrors.Errorf("got %q: %w", line, ErrCanceled)
   130	                }
   131	                if opts.Validate != nil {
   132	                        err := opts.Validate(line)
   133	                        if err != nil {
   134	                                _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout, pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Error, err.Error()))
   135	                                return Prompt(inv, opts)
   136	                        }
   137	                }
   138	                return line, nil
   139	        case <-inv.Context().Done():
   140	                return "", inv.Context().Err()
   141	        case <-interrupt:
   142	                // Print a newline so that any further output starts properly on a new line.
   143	                _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
   144	                return "", ErrCanceled
   145	        }
   146	}
   147	
   148	func promptJSON(reader io.Reader, line string) (string, error) {
   149	        var data bytes.Buffer
   150	        for {
   151	                _, _ = data.WriteString(line)
   152	                var rawMessage json.RawMessage
   153	                err := json.Unmarshal(data.Bytes(), &rawMessage)
   154	                if err != nil {
   155	                        if err.Error() != "unexpected end of JSON input" {
   156	                                // If a real syntax error occurs in JSON,
   157	                                // we want to return that partial line to the user.
   158	                                err = nil
   159	                                line = data.String()
   160	                                break
   161	                        }
   162	
   163	                        // Read line-by-line. We can't use a JSON decoder
   164	                        // here because it doesn't work by newline, so
   165	                        // reads will block.
   166	                        line, err = readUntil(reader, '\n')
   167	                        if err != nil {
   168	                                break
   169	                        }
   170	                        continue
   171	                }
   172	                // Compacting the JSON makes it easier for parsing and testing.
   173	                rawJSON := data.Bytes()
   174	                data.Reset()
   175	                err = json.Compact(&data, rawJSON)
   176	                if err != nil {
   177	                        return line, xerrors.Errorf("compact json: %w", err)
   178	                }
   179	                return data.String(), nil
   180	        }
   181	        return line, nil
   182	}
   183	
   184	// readUntil the first occurrence of delim in the input, returning a string containing the data up
   185	// to and including the delimiter. Unlike `bufio`, it only reads until the delimiter and no further
   186	// bytes. If readUntil encounters an error before finding a delimiter, it returns the data read
   187	// before the error and the error itself (often io.EOF). readUntil returns err != nil if and only if
   188	// the returned data does not end in delim.
   189	func readUntil(r io.Reader, delim byte) (string, error) {
   190	        var (
   191	                have []byte
   192	                b    = make([]byte, 1)
   193	        )
   194	        for {
   195	                n, err := r.Read(b)
   196	                if n > 0 {
   197	                        have = append(have, b[0])
   198	                        if b[0] == delim {
   199	                                // match `bufio` in that we only return non-nil if we didn't find the delimiter,
   200	                                // regardless of whether we also erred.
   201	                                return string(have), nil
   202	                        }
   203	                }
   204	                if err != nil {
   205	                        return string(have), err
   206	                }
   207	        }
   208	}
   209	
   210	// readSecretInput reads secret input from the terminal rune-by-rune,
   211	// masking each character with an asterisk.
   212	func readSecretInput(f *os.File, w io.Writer) (string, error) {
   213	        // Put terminal into raw mode (no echo, no line buffering).
   214	        oldState, err := pty.MakeInputRaw(f.Fd())
   215	        if err != nil {
   216	                return "", err
   217	        }
   218	        defer func() {
   219	                _ = pty.RestoreTerminal(f.Fd(), oldState)
   220	        }()
   221	
   222	        reader := bufio.NewReader(f)
   223	        var runes []rune
   224	
   225	        for {
   226	                r, _, err := reader.ReadRune()
   227	                if err != nil {
   228	                        return "", err
   229	                }
   230	
   231	                switch {
   232	                case r == '\r' || r == '\n':
   233	                        // Finish on Enter
   234	                        if _, err := fmt.Fprint(w, "\r\n"); err != nil {
   235	                                return "", err
   236	                        }
   237	                        return string(runes), nil
   238	
   239	                case r == 3:
   240	                        // Ctrl+C
   241	                        return "", ErrCanceled
   242	
   243	                case r == 127 || r == '\b':
   244	                        // Backspace/Delete: remove last rune
   245	                        if len(runes) > 0 {
   246	                                // Erase the last '*' on the screen
   247	                                if _, err := fmt.Fprint(w, "\b \b"); err != nil {
   248	                                        return "", err
   249	                                }
   250	                                runes = runes[:len(runes)-1]
   251	                        }
   252	
   253	                default:
   254	                        // Only mask printable, non-control runes
   255	                        if !unicode.IsControl(r) {
   256	                                runes = append(runes, r)
   257	                                if _, err := fmt.Fprint(w, "*"); err != nil {
   258	                                        return "", err
   259	                                }
   260	                        }
   261	                }
   262	        }
   263	}

				if len(option.Description) > 0 {

package cliui

import (
        "encoding/json"
        "fmt"
        "strings"

        "github.com/coder/coder/v2/codersdk"
        "github.com/coder/pretty"
        "github.com/coder/serpent"
)

func RichParameter(inv *serpent.Invocation, templateVersionParameter codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter, defaultOverrides map[string]string) (string, error) {
        label := templateVersionParameter.Name
        if templateVersionParameter.DisplayName != "" {
                label = templateVersionParameter.DisplayName
        }

        if templateVersionParameter.Ephemeral {
                label += pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Warn, " (build option)")
        }

        _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout, Bold(label))

        if templateVersionParameter.DescriptionPlaintext != "" {
                _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout, "  "+strings.TrimSpace(strings.Join(strings.Split(templateVersionParameter.DescriptionPlaintext, "\n"), "\n  "))+"\n")
        }

        defaultValue := templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue
        if v, ok := defaultOverrides[templateVersionParameter.Name]; ok {
                defaultValue = v
        }

        var err error
        var value string
        switch {
        case templateVersionParameter.Type == "list(string)":
                // Move the cursor up a single line for nicer display!
                _, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")

                var options []string
                err = json.Unmarshal([]byte(templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue), &options)
                if err != nil {
                        return "", err
                }

if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0 {
options = []string{}
for _, opt := range templateVersionParameter.Options {
options = append(options, opt.Value)
}
}

                values, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{
                        Options:  options,
                        Defaults: options,
                })
                if err == nil {
                        v, err := json.Marshal(&values)
                        if err != nil {
                                return "", err
                        }

                        _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
                        pretty.Fprintf(
                                inv.Stdout,
                                DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%s\n", strings.Join(values, ", "),
                        )
                        value = string(v)
                }
        case len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0:
                // Move the cursor up a single line for nicer display!
                _, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")
                var richParameterOption *codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption
                richParameterOption, err = RichSelect(inv, RichSelectOptions{
                        Options:    templateVersionParameter.Options,
                        Default:    defaultValue,
                        HideSearch: true,
                })
                if err == nil {
                        _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
                        pretty.Fprintf(inv.Stdout, DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%s\n", richParameterOption.Name)
                        value = richParameterOption.Value
                }
        default:
                text := "Enter a value"
                if !templateVersionParameter.Required {
                        text += fmt.Sprintf(" (default: %q)", defaultValue)
                }
                text += ":"

                value, err = Prompt(inv, PromptOptions{
                        Text: Bold(text),
                        Validate: func(value string) error {
                                return validateRichPrompt(value, templateVersionParameter)
                        },
                })
                value = strings.TrimSpace(value)
        }
        if err != nil {
                return "", err
        }

        // If they didn't specify anything, use the default value if set.
        if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) == 0 && value == "" {
                value = defaultValue
        }

        return value, nil
}

func validateRichPrompt(value string, p codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter) error {
        return codersdk.ValidateWorkspaceBuildParameter(p, &codersdk.WorkspaceBuildParameter{
                Name:  p.Name,
                Value: value,
        }, nil)
}

		_, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")

		var options []string
		_ = json.Unmarshal([]byte(defaultValue), &options)

		var defaults []string
		_ = json.Unmarshal([]byte(templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue), &defaults)

		if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0 {
			options = make([]string, len(templateVersionParameter.Options))
			for i, option := range templateVersionParameter.Options {
				line := option.Name
				if len(option.Description) > 0 {
					line += ": " + option.Description
				}
				options[i] = line
			}

			// We need to map the default values to their rich options.
			mappedDefaults := make([]string, 0, len(defaults))
			for _, dValue := range defaults {
				for i, option := range templateVersionParameter.Options {
					if option.Value == dValue {
						mappedDefaults = append(mappedDefaults, options[i])
						break
					}
				}
			}
			defaults = mappedDefaults
		}

		selectedOptions, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{
			Options:  options,
			Defaults: defaults,
		})
		if err == nil {
			if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0 {
				mappedSelected := make([]string, 0, len(selectedOptions))
				for _, selected := range selectedOptions {
					for i, option := range options {
						if option == selected {
							mappedSelected = append(mappedSelected, templateVersionParameter.Options[i].Value)
							break
						}
					}
				}
				selectedOptions = mappedSelected
			}

			v, err := json.Marshal(&selectedOptions)
			if err != nil {
				return "", err
			}

			_, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
			pretty.Fprintf(
				inv.Stdout,
				DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%s\n", strings.Join(selectedOptions, ", "),
			)
			value = string(v)

🎬 ACTION
printf 'package cliui

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"strings"

	"github.com/coder/coder/v2/codersdk"
	"github.com/coder/pretty"
	"github.com/coder/serpent"
)

func RichParameter(inv *serpent.Invocation, templateVersionParameter codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter, defaultOverrides map[string]string) (string, error) {
	label := templateVersionParameter.Name
	if templateVersionParameter.DisplayName != "" {
		label = templateVersionParameter.DisplayName
	}

	if templateVersionParameter.Ephemeral {
		label += pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Warn, " (build option)")
	}

	_, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout, Bold(label))

	if templateVersionParameter.DescriptionPlaintext != "" {
		_, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout, "  "+strings.TrimSpace(strings.Join(strings.Split(templateVersionParameter.DescriptionPlaintext, "\n"), "\n  "))+"\n")
	}

	defaultValue := templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue
	if v, ok := defaultOverrides[templateVersionParameter.Name]; ok {
		defaultValue = v
	}

	var err error
	var value string
	switch {
	case templateVersionParameter.Type == "list(string)":
		// Move the cursor up a single line for nicer display!
		_, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")

		var options []string
		_ = json.Unmarshal([]byte(defaultValue), &options)

		var defaults []string
		_ = json.Unmarshal([]byte(templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue), &defaults)

		if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0 {
			options = make([]string, len(templateVersionParameter.Options))
			for i, option := range templateVersionParameter.Options {
				line := option.Name
				if len(option.Description) > 0 {
					line += ": " + option.Description
				}
				options[i] = line
			}

			// We need to map the default values to their rich options.
			mappedDefaults := make([]string, 0, len(defaults))
			for _, dValue := range defaults {
				for i, option := range templateVersionParameter.Options {
					if option.Value == dValue {
						mappedDefaults = append(mappedDefaults, options[i])
						break
					}
				}
			}
			defaults = mappedDefaults
		}

		selectedOptions, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{
			Options:  options,
			Defaults: defaults,
		})
		if err == nil {
			if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0 {
				mappedSelected := make([]string, 0, len(selectedOptions))
				for _, selected := range selectedOptions {
					for i, option := range options {
						if option == selected {
							mappedSelected = append(mappedSelected, templateVersionParameter.Options[i].Value)
							break
						}
					}
				}
				selectedOptions = mappedSelected
			}

			v, err := json.Marshal(&selectedOptions)
			if err != nil {
				return "", err
			}

			_, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
			pretty.Fprintf(
				inv.Stdout,
				DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%%s\n", strings.Join(selectedOptions, ", "),
			)
			value = string(v)
		}
	case len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0:
		// Move the cursor up a single line for nicer display!
		_, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")
		var richParameterOption *codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption
		richParameterOption, err = RichSelect(inv, RichSelectOptions{
			Options:    templateVersionParameter.Options,
			Default:    defaultValue,
			HideSearch: true,
		})
		if err == nil {
			_, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
			pretty.Fprintf(inv.Stdout, DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%%s\n", richParameterOption.Name)
			value = richParameterOption.Value
		}
	default:
		text := \"Enter a value\"
		if !templateVersionParameter.Required {
			text += fmt.Sprintf(\" (default: %%q)\", defaultValue)
		}
		text += \":\"

		value, err = Prompt(inv, PromptOptions{
			Text: Bold(text),
			Validate: func(value string) error {
				return validateRichPrompt(value, templateVersionParameter)
			},
		})
		value = strings.TrimSpace(value)
	}
	if err != nil {
		return \"\", err
	}

	// If they didn't specify anything, use the default value if set.
	if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) == 0 && value == \"\" {
		value = defaultValue
	}

	return value, nil
}

func validateRichPrompt(value string, p codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter) error {
	return codersdk.ValidateWorkspaceBuildParameter(p, &codersdk.WorkspaceBuildParameter{
		Name:  p.Name,
		Value: value,
	}, nil)
}

import sys

with open('/testbed/cli/cliui/parameter.go', 'r') as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

new_lines = []
skip = False
for line in lines:
    if 'case templateVersionParameter.Type == \"list(string)\":' in line:
        new_lines.append(line)
        new_lines.append('\t\t// Move the cursor up a single line for nicer display!\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t_, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, \"\\033[1A\")\n')
        new_lines.append('\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\tvar options []string\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t_ = json.Unmarshal([]byte(defaultValue), &options)\n')
        new_lines.append('\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\tvar defaults []string\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t_ = json.Unmarshal([]byte(templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue), &defaults)\n')
        new_lines.append('\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\tif len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0 {\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\toptions = make([]string, len(templateVersionParameter.Options))\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\tfor i, option := range templateVersionParameter.Options {\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\tline := option.Name\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\tif len(option.Description) > 0 {\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\t\tline += \": \" + option.Description\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\t}\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\toptions[i] = line\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t}\n')
        new_lines.append('\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\tmappedDefaults := make([]string, 0, len(defaults))\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\tfor _, dValue := range defaults {\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\tfor i, option := range templateVersionParameter.Options {\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\t\tif option.Value == dValue {\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\t\t\tmappedDefaults = append(mappedDefaults, options[i])\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\t\t}\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\t}\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t}\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\tdefaults = mappedDefaults\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t}\n')
        new_lines.append('\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\tselectedOptions, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\tOptions:  options,\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\tDefaults: defaults,\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t})\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\tif err == nil {\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\tif len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0 {\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\tmappedSelected := make([]string, 0, len(selectedOptions))\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\tfor _, selected := range selectedOptions {\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\t\tfor i, option := range options {\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\t\t\tif option == selected {\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\t\t\t\tmappedSelected = append(mappedSelected, templateVersionParameter.Options[i].Value)\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\t\t}\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\t}\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\tselectedOptions = mappedSelected\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t}\n')
        new_lines.append('\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\tv, err := json.Marshal(&selectedOptions)\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\tif err != nil {\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\treturn \"\", err\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t}\n')
        new_lines.append('\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t_, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\tpretty.Fprintf(\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\tinv.Stdout,\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t\tDefaultStyles.Prompt, \"%s\\n\", strings.Join(selectedOptions, \", \"),\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\t)\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t\tvalue = string(v)\n')
        new_lines.append('\t\t}\n')
        skip = True
    elif skip and 'case len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0:' in line:
        skip = False
        new_lines.append(line)
    elif not skip:
        new_lines.append(line)

with open('/testbed/cli/cliui/parameter.go', 'w') as f:
    f.writelines(new_lines)

        case templateVersionParameter.Type == "list(string)":
		// Move the cursor up a single line for nicer display!
		_, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")

		var options []string
		_ = json.Unmarshal([]byte(defaultValue), &options)

		var defaults []string
		_ = json.Unmarshal([]byte(templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue), &defaults)

		if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0 {
			options = make([]string, len(templateVersionParameter.Options))
			for i, option := range templateVersionParameter.Options {
				line := option.Name
				if len(option.Description) > 0 {
					line += ": " + option.Description
				}
				options[i] = line
			}

			mappedDefaults := make([]string, 0, len(defaults))
			for _, dValue := range defaults {
				for i, option := range templateVersionParameter.Options {
					if option.Value == dValue {
						mappedDefaults = append(mappedDefaults, options[i])
						break
					}
				}
			}
			defaults = mappedDefaults
		}

		selectedOptions, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{
			Options:  options,
			Defaults: defaults,
		})
		if err == nil {
			if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0 {
				mappedSelected := make([]string, 0, len(selectedOptions))
				for _, selected := range selectedOptions {
					for i, option := range options {
						if option == selected {
							mappedSelected = append(mappedSelected, templateVersionParameter.Options[i].Value)
							break
						}
					}
				}
				selectedOptions = mappedSelected
			}

			v, err := json.Marshal(&selectedOptions)
			if err != nil {
				return "", err
			}

			_, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
			pretty.Fprintf(
				inv.Stdout,
				DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%s\n", strings.Join(selectedOptions, ", ")
			)
			value = string(v)
		}

                        Options:    templateVersionParameter.Options,
                        Default:    defaultValue,
                        HideSearch: true,
                })

                        _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)

                        value = richParameterOption.Value

        default:

+import sys
+
+with open('/testbed/cli/cliui/parameter.go', 'r') as f:
+    lines = f.readlines()
+
+new_lines = []
+for line in lines:

+        new_lines.append(line.replace('strings.Join(selectedOptions, ", ")', 'strings.Join(selectedOptions, ", "),'))
+    else:
+        new_lines.append(line)
+
+with open('/testbed/cli/cliui/parameter.go', 'w') as f:
+    f.writelines(new_lines)
